\subsection{Detailed Description}
Author\-: Matthew Horridge\par
 The University Of Manchester\par
 Bio-\/\-Health Informatics Group\par
 Date\-: 10-\/\-Sep-\/2007\par
 \par
 

A parser for the Manchester O\-W\-L Syntax. All properties must be defined before they are used. For example, consider the restriction has\-Part some Leg. The parser must know in advance whether or not has\-Part is an object property or a data property so that Leg gets parsed correctly. In a tool, such as an editor, it is expected that has\-Part will already exists as either a data property or an object property. If a complete ontology is being parsed, it is expected that has\-Part will have been defined at the top of the file before it is used in any class expressions or property assertions (e.\-g. Object\-Property\-: has\-Part)
